\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__hypotests_8py_source_l00630}00630\ \ \ \ \ t\ =\ n*(n+1)/2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__hypotests_8py_source_l00631}00631\ \ \ \ \ q\ =\ 2*t}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__hypotests_8py_source_l00632}00632\ \ \ \ \ j\ =\ np.arange(q)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__hypotests_8py_source_l00633}00633\ \ \ \ \ theta\ =\ 2*np.pi/q*j}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__hypotests_8py_source_l00634}00634\ \ \ \ \ phi\_sp\ =\ np.prod(np.cos(theta*ai),\ axis=0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__hypotests_8py_source_l00635}00635\ \ \ \ \ phi\_s\ =\ np.exp(1j*theta*t)\ *\ phi\_sp}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__hypotests_8py_source_l00636}00636\ \ \ \ \ p\ =\ np.real(ifft(phi\_s))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__hypotests_8py_source_l00637}00637\ \ \ \ \ res\ =\ np.zeros(int(t)+1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__hypotests_8py_source_l00638}00638\ \ \ \ \ res[:-\/1:]\ =\ p[::2]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__hypotests_8py_source_l00639}00639\ \ \ \ \ res[0]\ /=\ 2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__hypotests_8py_source_l00640}00640\ \ \ \ \ res[-\/1]\ =\ res[0]}
